TxtCollectShine	Collect more Power Moons!
TxtCaption00_Sand	Home of Red Sands and Lively Locals.
TxtRegionCaption_Sand	Gateway to the stark beauty of the desert.
TxtData01_Sand	Middling\nExpansive\nTostarenans, Moe-Eyes
TxtData02_Sand	Pyramid-shaped\nTourism, precious stones\nAverage 104℉
TxtTitle01_Sand	Tostarenan Tourism
TxtContents01_Sand	A small town that serves as the hub\nfor tourists planning to visit the\nInverted Pyramid. The colorful\nbuildings and cheerful people\nprovide a warm welcome for visitors.\nThey're happy to provide direction,\nso don't hesitate to say hello.
TxtCaption01_Sand	The bright colors of Tostarena.
TxtTitle02_Sand	Mysterious Ancient Ruins
TxtContents02_Sand	Head north from town and you'll be\ngreeted by ancient ruins that dot the\nexpansive desert. Though many have\nbecome conflict regions patrolled by\nBullet Bills, their status as important\nheritage sites is undeniable.\n\nYour eye will be drawn to the large\nstone tower at the heart of the ruins.\nDue to extensive hollowing\nunderground, quicksand has become\nprevalent in this area, so watch out.
TxtCaption02_Sand	The ruins greet you with an impressive gate.
TxtTitle03_Sand	Inverted Pyramid
TxtContents03_Sand	The true "can't miss" of this region,\nthe Inverted Pyramid may look\nunstable, but rest assured it never\ntopples and has thrilled tourists\nfor years. It is said that a legendary\nartifact called the Binding Band lies\nwithin, and the upside-down\npyramid symbolizes how those\njoined by it will never part even\nif the world turns upside down.
TxtCaption03_Sand	Like a precious gem itself.
TxtTitle04_Sand	Jaxi
TxtContents04_Sand	Let's have a look at the curious local\ntransport method known as the Jaxi.\n\nJust hop on the back of one, and\nas you might guess from their\nappearance, you'll be in for a wild\nbut completely reliable ride.\n\nMake good use of them and you'll\nbe exploring this unforgiving\ndesert in comfort and style.
TxtCaption04_Sand	Payment required in advance.
TxtTitle05_Sand	Living Heart of the Desert
TxtContents05_Sand	Here's a spot to moisten your dried\nand withered heart, with greenery\nand water to make you forget you're\nin the desert. The fish and birds\nare plentiful and well worth a visit.
TxtCaption05_Sand	So beautiful you'll think you're at a resort.
TxtCaption06_Sand	The Moe-Eyes love their shades.\nThey'll run if chased, but they're a proud people who have long\ninhabited these ruins. Please be polite.
TxtContents07_Sand	1．Enjoy the small but lively desert village and its charming inhabitants.\n2．Wonder at the Inverted Pyramid and its upside-down magic.\n3．Watch for the gem iconography carved in relief on the ruins.
TxtCaption00_Forest	Ancient Gardens Tended by Futuristic Machines
TxtRegionCaption_Forest	The world's most advanced greenhouse.
TxtData01_Forest	Automated\nDeep, Wide\nSteam Gardeners
TxtData02_Forest	Nut-shaped\nFlowers\nAverage 82℉
TxtTitle01_Forest	The Living Factory
TxtContents01_Forest	No one knows who built the giant\nmachines dotting this land, but today\nthe Steam Gardeners use them to\nmaintain the greatest flower gardens\nin the world. The giant dome is\nclimate-controlled and apparently\nself-sufficient, operating with no\nmaintenance since ancient times.
TxtCaption01_Forest	You can't miss the bright red machinery.
TxtTitle02_Forest	Guardians of Paradise
TxtContents02_Forest	Visitors are welcomed not only by\nthe humid air, but worker robots\ntending the flowers. They're known as\nSteam Gardeners, longtime residents\nof the kingdom. You'll be impressed\nat how long they can work without\nrest, maintaining themselves perfectly.\nBut beyond being hard workers, the\nrobots love flowers—some grow\nthem right out of their heads! You'll\nfeel the Steam Gardeners' warm\nhearts, from their flowers and also\ntheir internal steam pumps.
TxtCaption02_Forest	Locals are a bit off-putting but quite friendly.
TxtTitle03_Forest	Flowers as a Way of Life
TxtContents03_Forest	While you'll see amazing flowers on\nany visit, you might be lucky enough\nto see the famous Steam Gardens\nSoir\xe9e Bouquet. It features giant white\nflowers that charm all who lay eyes\non it. As you might guess from the\nname, it's by far the most popular\nbouquet for wedding ceremonies,\nsought after by wedding planners\nthe world over.
TxtCaption03_Forest	There are flower gardens everywhere.
TxtTitle04_Forest	A Deep Wood's Secret
TxtContents04_Forest	It doesn't appear on any tours, but\nthere is an area untouched by the\nmachines of the Steam Gardens.\nHere the trees grow thickly, barely\nallowing any light through. The\nSteam Gardeners do not speak of it,\nbut rumor has it that they discourage\nvisiting this place because of the\ndanger posed by the giant creatures\nthat call it home.
TxtCaption04_Forest	Bring a pith helmet if you go exploring here!
TxtTitle05_Forest	A Growing Walkway
TxtContents05_Forest	Be sure to try the system of paths\ncalled the Flower Road. You'll marvel\nat plants growing into temporary but\nwalkable bridges. Watch your step,\nthough—nature has no handrails.
TxtCaption05_Forest	Safety tip: Don't dawdle.
TxtCaption06_Forest	Birds NOT of a Feather\nLocal birds here seem remarkably fond of their mechanical neighbors.
TxtContents07_Forest	1. Smell the flowers. Not that you can miss them, but do savor the scent.\n2. Admire the Steam Gardeners and their impressive devotion to their work.\n3. Appreciate machines and nature living in exquisite harmony.
TxtCaption00_Clash	Remote Island Chain in the Tropics
TxtRegionCaption_Clash	Lively paradise surrounded by a sea of death.
TxtData01_Clash	Unknown\nSmallish\nUnknown
TxtData02_Clash	Leaf-shaped\nUnknown\nAverage 91℉
TxtTitle01_Clash	A Dense, Primeval Forest
TxtContents01_Clash	Few visit these remote islands\nsurrounded by poison, but they are\ndense with plants that have followed\na unique evolutionary path. There is\na strange unity between the vibrantly\ncolored plants, the odd animals, and\nthe sea of poison surrounding them.
TxtCaption01_Clash	Splendid flora breathes life into this place.
TxtTitle02_Clash	Nature's Traffic Lights
TxtContents02_Clash	The Tropical Wigglers found here are\nnot aggressive and are mostly genial\nand pleasant creatures. You should,\nhowever, avoid touching them, for\nsafety's sake. They stretch and\ncontract their bodies constantly\nand have a habit of stretching across\nmajor pathways, so you may need\nto wait for the right moment to pass.\nThis behavior has given them the\nnickname "traffic lights of the island."\nBe sure to look both ways before\nyou cross.
TxtCaption02_Clash	Some local species are quite colorful.
TxtTitle03_Clash	Thief of the Skies
TxtContents03_Clash	The undisputed ruler of the skies here\nis the Klepto. This large bird has keen\neyesight that enables it to spot prey\nfrom far above before swooping\ndown to snatch it up in an instant.\nOnce ensnared in its sharp claws,\nescape is quite difficult, and many\nsmaller visitors have been carried\noff in this way.
TxtCaption03_Clash	It even LOOKS evil.
TxtTitle04_Clash	Ruins Steeped in Mystery
TxtContents04_Clash	The purpose of the distinctive ruins\nscattered throughout the island\nremains unclear. The starburst pattern\nthat appears on them MAY indicate\na spot capable of withstanding a\ngreat impact. The builders clearly\nmastered stonework, as these\nstructures still operate and move\nperhaps centuries after their creators\nhad disappeared.
TxtCaption04_Clash	The exact mechanism is not yet understood.
TxtTitle05_Clash	Watch Those Hands
TxtContents05_Clash	The Trapeetle is a local hazard. Its\nlarge hands capture prey, who are\nheld tight as the creature explodes\nin a tragic display seen absolutely\nnowhere else in nature. Best to avoid.
TxtCaption05_Clash	The so-called "guardians of the ruins."
TxtCaption06_Clash	A Symbol from Ancient Times\nNow seen all over the world, this starburst symbol is thought to have originated\non these islands. But what does it communicate? The mystery may never be solved.
TxtContents07_Clash	1. Enjoy the breathtaking scenery, but beware the death-dealing poison.\n2. Watch the Tropical Wiggler grow and shrink—it is simply mesmerizing.\n3. Puzzle over the odd mechanics of these strange ruins.
TxtCaption00_City	Modern Commerce Center and Urban Playground
TxtRegionCaption_City	The city that never leaps.
TxtData01_City	Crowded\nRidonkulous\nNew Donkers
TxtData02_City	Portrait-stamped\nInformation, Ads\nAverage 81℉
TxtTitle01_City	Scraping the Sky
TxtContents01_City	The skyscrapers of New Donk City\nare most people's first association\nwith the city. But even among those,\nNew Donk City Hall stands out as \nthe very symbol of this great city,\nso don't miss it. Who knows, you\nmight even run into world-renowned\nMayor Pauline!
TxtCaption01_City	New Donk City Hall and Mayor Pauline.
TxtTitle02_City	A Million-Coin View
TxtContents02_City	If you've come to New Donk City, you\nowe it to yourself to see it at night.\nThe best viewing spot is the\nlandmark New Donk City Hall, but\nsadly the interior is closed for\nconstruction, so you'll have to aim\nfor one of the neighboring buildings.\n\nIf it's festival season, you'll have a\nchance at a once-in-a-lifetime\nexperience, but the timing is a bit\nirregular, so be sure to check the\nschedule beforehand.
TxtCaption02_City	The nighttime skyline shines from any angle.
TxtTitle03_City	Crazy Cap Flagship Store
TxtContents03_City	There's probably only one brand that\nthe entire world knows, and that's\nCrazy Cap. Their original flagship\nstore is right here in New Donk City.\n\nThe unique storefront is converted\nfrom an old theater. Theater space\nis no longer much in demand, with\nso many street performers in the city.
TxtCaption03_City	The world's most trusted brand in headwear.
TxtTitle04_City	Always Be Constructing
TxtContents04_City	New Donkers are used to\nconstruction and new developments.\nThere's always work being done\nbelow ground, on rooftops, and\ninside buildings, so power lines\nnever get taken down—they run\nthroughout town.\n\nUnaccustomed travelers should\nwatch out for the cranes, girders,\nand manholes scattered everywhere.
TxtCaption04_City	There aren't even safety rails.
TxtTitle05_City	Scooting Across Town
TxtContents05_City	These motor scooters may look\nold-fashioned, but they pack a punch\nand are perfect for tooling around\nthe city. Be sure to try one out!
